Members of the Company&#8217;s senior leadership team discussed the Company&#8217;s plans to leverage its industry-leading network to unlock future growth from its existing and new businesses over the next three years. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The event is accessible via webcast on the Company&#8217;s Investor Relations website <span style="white-space:nowrap">at&#160;http://investor.t-mobile.com.&#160;A</span> replay of the webcast along with presentation materials will be available on the Investor Relations website at the conclusion of the event. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">A copy of the press release relating to the Capital Markets Day is attached hereto as Exhibit 99.1. <HTML><HEAD>
<TITLE>EX-99.1</TITLE>
</HEAD>
 <BODY BGCOLOR="WHITE" STYLE="line-height:Normal">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>EXHIBIT 99.1 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Fueled by Network Leadership and Transformative <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">AI-Enabled</FONT> Customer Experiences, <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> Outlines Ambitious Plan for Continued Growth Leadership, Value Creation and Share Taking in Wireless and Broadband While Growing New Businesses </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><I>Profitable customer growth strategy expected to deliver outsized financial growth, including accelerating growth in Service Revenues, a
nearly $10&nbsp;billion increase in Annual Core Adjusted EBITDA by 2027,<SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP> and industry-leading Adjusted Free Cash Flow margin </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>SAN FRANCISCO &#150; September</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;18, 2024</B> &#150; At its Capital Markets Day event today,
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> US, Inc. (NASDAQ: TMUS) unveiled an ambitious three-year plan that demonstrates how the company will continue its growth momentum to unlock massive value creation into the future. <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> senior leadership team shared a clear strategy for how the company will achieve success in the years ahead centered around the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Un-carrier&#146;s</FONT> proven
network, value and leading customer experience, including how it will extend its network leadership by continuing its transformation into an <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">AI-enabled,</FONT> data-informed, digital-first organization. The company
expects continued profitable share gains across underpenetrated segments, sees continued industry leading growth in its broadband business, outlined a framework for new future revenue opportunities, and more. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The plan builds on <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> track record of providing value for consumers while delivering phenomenal business
results. The company not only met but completely surpassed the ambitious goals it set at its previous Capital Markets Day in 2021 &#150; building America&#146;s best network, expanding its addressable markets, and unlocking $8&nbsp;billion in run
rate synergies from the Sprint merger, all while delivering financial results that exceeded expectations, including over $30&nbsp;billion of cumulative Adjusted Free Cash Flow<SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP> from 2020 through
2023. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">&#147;T-Mobile</FONT> is a company on the move with tremendous opportunities in front of us to further extend our
outperformance in customer growth and translate that into strong top and bottom-line growth that will enable a compelling capital return opportunity over the next few years,&#148; said <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> CEO Mike
Sievert. &#147;As the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Un-carrier</FONT> we have always set big goals, and our track record over the last four years shows that we deliver on them. Now we&#146;re tapping into this momentum and dreaming even bigger
for the next era of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Un-carrier,</FONT> championing new standards for customer experiences, how networks are built and beyond. The opportunity in front of us is huge and we can&#146;t wait to capture it.&#148; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The next era of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> profitable growth leadership will focus on key differentiators that will collectively
unlock outsized financial results and stockholder returns: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Extending Network Leadership</B><B> </B><B>&#150;</B> <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT>
announced plans to not just defend, but extend its multi-year network leadership position enabled by the company&#146;s industry-best assets, an innovative Customer-Driven Coverage (CDC) approach to network investments, and further technology
deployments including Massive <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Multiple-input/multiple-out</FONT> (Massive MIMO), Voice over New Radio (VoNR), four-carrier aggregation and the U.S.&#146;s first broad deployment of 5G Advanced - all enabled by the
only scaled nationwide 5G standalone network. The company also announced a <U>collaboration with NVIDIA, Ericsson and Nokia</U> to invest in an industry-first <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">AI-RAN</FONT> (radio access network) Innovation Center
focused on bringing RAN and AI innovation closer together to deliver transformational network experiences &#150; all while maintaining its network advantage and laying the groundwork for the future.
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">best-in-class</FONT></FONT> spectrum and network resources, customer-first focus, and leadership in deploying the latest
network technologies will remain at the core of its growth formula. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> has the deepest <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-6GHz</FONT> spectrum holdings and the lowest frequency across each layer of the
network including <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">low-band,</FONT> <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mid-band</FONT> and even mmWave. This gives the company propagation advantages that are unmatched across the industry, deployed across a dense
network grid, rooted in its <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mid-band</FONT> spectrum layer from day one, delivering an unrivaled consistency of experience with the best 5G availability by more than five times that of the closest competitor,
<U>according to Opensignal</U>, and speeds that are more than 2 times faster, <U>according to Ookla</U>. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Transformative Customer Experiences &#150; </B>Leveraging the latest AI technology and digital capabilities,
the company will continue transforming its approach to customer experiences. Wireless is one of the remaining industries that is not fully digital, but the company sees an opportunity to change that through tools like its <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Life</FONT> app, which can effectively tap into customer preferences and radically simplify their experiences. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> aims to ultimately enable 100% of upgrades and the majority
of customer activations to be done digitally. The company is also <U>joining forces with global technology leader OpenAI</U> to custom-build IntentCX, a predictive AI platform that will revolutionize customer engagement, better anticipating and
proactively solving customer issues, offering self-service options and taking actions on customers&#146; behalf. These efforts should reduce inbound customer contacts to Care by 75%, while increasing satisfaction and significantly lower operating
costs. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">We are not able to forecast Net income on a forward-looking basis without unreasonable efforts due to the high
variability and difficulty in predicting certain items that affect Net income, including, but not limited to, Income tax expense and Interest expense. Core Adjusted EBITDA should not be used to predict Net income as the difference between this
measure and Net income is variable. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Adjusted Free Cash Flow for 2020 is combined and adjusted due to the timing of the closing of the Sprint merger
and excludes gross payments for the settlement of interest rate swaps. See &#147;Reconciliation of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Financial Measures to GAAP Financial Measures&#148; </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Profitable Share Taking &#150;</B> <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> plans to consistently and
profitably grow its core wireless business with continued share taking across underpenetrated markets and deeper customer relationships through its portfolio of products and services. The company has even more room to run in Smaller Markets and
Rural Areas (SMRA), where its &#147;win share&#148; is now #1, and significantly above the company&#146;s market share, on the strength of its extensive value and 5G network leadership. In addition, Top 100 Markets continue to be a significant
growth driver, as the company remains underpenetrated among those shopping primarily on network, or &#147;network seekers&#148;, the company is posting consistent growth, building its overall market lead, while network reputation rapidly improves,
demonstrating significant room to run. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> also remains underpenetrated in 30% of Top 100 Markets, where its market share is in third place, representing a growth opportunity that is more like SMRA. <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> for Business (TFB) has transformed from a provider of basic cell phone service to a strategic solutions organization and continues to be a growth engine with significant momentum. Its next phase of growth
will come from deploying enhanced digital tools, extending its leadership across small to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mid-market</FONT> companies, and continuing to deliver advanced solutions to Enterprise and Government customers. With this
strategy, the company expects TFB will deliver double-digit service revenue compound annual growth rate from 2023 to 2027. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Leading Broadband Growth</B> &#150; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> will continue its
industry leading Broadband growth by scaling its national, yet hyper-local <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">go-to-market</FONT></FONT> playbook to serve more customers and create revenue opportunities. The company
aims to reach 12&nbsp;million 5G broadband customers by 2028 using excess capacity, a more than 50% increase from its previous target of 7 to 8&nbsp;million customers by 2025. Fiber to the home will augment the company&#146;s 5G broadband success,
providing an accretive and complementary opportunity to deliver connectivity to even more Americans. With a 5G broadband waitlist of more than 1&nbsp;million potential customers, combined with its brand, distribution, and existing customer base, <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> can achieve lower cost to acquire new customers, lower cost to serve, and faster and deeper penetration curves enabling greater returns. The company expects to reach 12 to 15&nbsp;million or more households
passed by the end of 2030 with its fiber partnerships and expects to realize an <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">all-in</FONT> internal rate of return of around 20%, and potentially higher, from its fiber joint ventures. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Growing New Businesses &#150; </B>Using its unique assets and by leveraging its embedded customer
relationships, broad distribution, strong brand affinity, and the most advanced 5G network, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> will unlock opportunities that meet clear customer needs in new areas. One example is in the advertising
space, where <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> grew an opportunity to market solutions that it built to improve advertising in its own business to other advertisers into an over $1&nbsp;billion in annual revenue business. Another
example is <U><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Priority</FONT></U>, which gives first responder agencies of all sizes priority on the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> network to help ensure <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">best-in-class</FONT></FONT> connectivity during times of congestion, especially massive emergencies, and offers support for a wide range of data-intensive applications. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Outsized Financial Growth</B> <B>&#150; </B><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> has delivered
industry leading growth across customers, service revenues, and profitability, translating those wins into what matters the most: the industry&#146;s best Adjusted Free Cash Flow margin.<B> </B>Combining the key differentiators will result in
continued industry leading growth in profitability and Adjusted Free Cash Flow conversion, and a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">best-in-class</FONT></FONT> balance sheet, while enabling smart investments and
driving outsized stockholder returns. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> 2027 guidance excludes pending acquisitions of UScellular, Metronet, and Lumos: </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Service revenue growth is anticipated to accelerate at a compound annual growth rate of approximately 5% at the
midpoint from 2023 to 2027, as the company expects to deliver $75 to $76&nbsp;billion in 2027. This is driven by continued wireless and broadband customer growth, continued growth in average revenue per account from deepening customer relationships
and growth in new businesses. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

$39&nbsp;billion in 2027, a compound annual growth rate of approximately 7% at the midpoint from 2023 to 2027, and an increase of approximately $10&nbsp;billion compared to 2023 at the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">high-end</FONT> of guidance.
This is expected to be driven by the operating leverage from its profitable growth model and enhanced with further significant operating efficiencies through technology innovation, AI, and digital leadership. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile,</FONT> Metro by <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> and Mint Mobile. For more information please visit: <U><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">https://www.t-mobile.com</FONT></U>. </P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Reconciliation of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Financial Measures to GAAP Financial Measures </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>(Unaudited) </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">This release includes <FONT

GAAP. Reconciliations for the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures to the most directly comparable GAAP financial measures are provided below. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> is not able to forecast
Net income on a forward-looking basis without unreasonable efforts due to the high variability and difficulty in predicting certain items that affect GAAP net income, including, but not limited to, Income tax expense and Interest expense. Adjusted
EBITDA and Core Adjusted EBITDA should not be used to predict Net income, as the difference between either of these measures and Net income is variable. </P>

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(1)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Combined net cash provided by operating activities, as adjusted, represents the summation of the GAAP measure
net cash provided by operating activities for <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> and Sprint aligned to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> accounting policies by adding historical capital expenditures for leased
devices, which <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> treats as an operating activity. Historical Sprint activity related to capital expenditures for leased devices has been reclassified to net cash provided by operating activities from
cash purchases of property and equipment within Net cash used in investing activities. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Definition of Terms </B></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>1.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left"><B>Adjusted EBITDA and Core Adjusted EBITDA</B> - Adjusted EBITDA represents earnings before Interest expense,
net of Interest income, Income tax expense, Depreciation and amortization, stock-based compensation and certain expenses, gains and losses which are not reflective of our ongoing operating performance (&#147;Special Items&#148;). Special Items
include Merger-related costs, including network decommissioning costs, incremental costs directly attributable to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19,</FONT> impairment expense, loss (gain) on disposal groups held for sale, certain
legal-related recoveries and expenses, restructuring costs not directly attributable to the Merger (including severance) and other <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-core</FONT> gains and losses. Core Adjusted EBITDA represents Adjusted EBITDA
less device lease revenues. Adjusted EBITDA and Core Adjusted EBITDA are <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures utilized by our management to monitor the financial performance of our operations. We historically used
Adjusted EBITDA and we currently use Core Adjusted EBITDA internally as a measure to evaluate and compensate our personnel and management for their performance. We use Adjusted EBITDA and Core Adjusted EBITDA as benchmarks to evaluate our operating
performance in comparison to our competitors. Management believes analysts and investors use Adjusted EBITDA and Core Adjusted EBITDA as supplemental measures to evaluate overall operating performance and to facilitate comparisons with other
wireless communications services companies because they are indicative of our ongoing operating performance and trends by excluding the impact of interest expense from financing, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> depreciation and
amortization from capital investments, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> stock-based compensation, and Special Items. Management believes analysts and investors use Core Adjusted EBITDA because it normalizes for the transition in the
Company&#146;s device financing strategy, by excluding the impact of device lease revenues from Adjusted EBITDA, to align with the exclusion of the related depreciation expense on leased devices from Adjusted EBITDA. Adjusted EBITDA and Core
Adjusted EBITDA have limitations as analytical tools and should not be considered in isolation or as substitutes for income from operations, net income or any other measure of financial performance reported in accordance with GAAP.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>2.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left"><B>Adjusted Free Cash Flow</B> - Net cash provided by operating activities less cash payments for purchases of
property and equipment, plus proceeds from sales of tower sites and proceeds related to beneficial interests in securitization transactions and less Cash payments for debt prepayment or debt extinguishment costs. Adjusted Free Cash Flow is utilized
by <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> management, investors, and analysts of our financial information to evaluate cash available to pay debt, repurchase shares, pay dividends and provide further investment in the business.
Starting in Q1 2023, we renamed Free Cash Flow to Adjusted Free Cash Flow. This change in name did not result in any change to the definition or calculation of this <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE>
</DIV></Center>
